path: Website/.github/workflows/generate-rss.yml
contents:
name: Generate RSS Feed
on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main
  workflow_dispatch:

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      contents: write
    steps:
      - name: Checkout code
        uses: actions/checkout@v4
        with:
          fetch-depth: 0

      - name: Set up Python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: '3.x'

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: pip install pyyaml

      - name: Generate RSS
        run: |
          python - <<EOF
          import yaml
          import os
          from xml.sax.saxutils import escape
          import datetime

          # Ensure directory exists
          os.makedirs('storage/internal', exist_ok=True)

          with open('storage/data/blogs.yaml', 'r') as f:
              data = yaml.safe_load(f)

          rss = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?>\n'
          rss += '<rss version="2.0" xmlns:atom="http://www.w3.org/2005/Atom">\n'
          rss += '<channel>\n'
          rss += '  <title>Error Dev - Blogs</title>\n'
          rss += '  <link>https://devicals.github.io/#page=blogs</link>\n'
          rss += '  <description>Latest updates from Error Dev</description>\n'
          rss += '  <atom:link href="https://devicals.github.io/storage/internal/blogs.xml" rel="self" type="application/rss+xml" />\n'

          if data and 'blogs' in data:
              for blog in data['blogs']:
                  # Convert DD/MM/YYYY to RSS date format (RFC 822)
                  try:
                      date_obj = datetime.datetime.strptime(blog['date'], '%d/%m/%Y')
                      pub_date = date_obj.strftime('%a, %d %b %Y 00:00:00 +0000')
                  except:
                      pub_date = datetime.datetime.now().strftime('%a, %d %b %Y 00:00:00 +0000')

                  rss += '  <item>\n'
                  rss += f'    <title>{escape(str(blog["title"]))}</title>\n'
                  rss += f'    <link>https://devicals.github.io/#page=blogs&amp;id={blog["id"]}</link>\n'
                  rss += f'    <guid isPermaLink="false">blog-id-{blog["id"]}</guid>\n'
                  rss += f'    <pubDate>{pub_date}</pub_date>\n'
                  # Clean up content for description
                  clean_content = blog["content"].replace('\n', ' ')[:200]
                  rss += f'    <description>{escape(clean_content)}...</description>\n'
                  rss += '  </item>\n'

          rss += '</channel>\n</rss>'

          with open('storage/internal/blogs.xml', 'w') as f:
              f.write(rss)
          EOF

      - name: Commit and Push
        run: |
          git config --global user.name "github-actions[bot]"
          git config --global user.email "github-actions[bot]@users.noreply.github.com"
          git add storage/internal/blogs.xml
          # Only commit if there are changes
          if git diff --staged --quiet; then
            echo "No changes to RSS feed."
          else
            git commit -m "Auto-generate RSS feed"
            git push origin main --force
          fi
---
path: Website/.github/workflows/get-stats.yml
contents:
name: Update Repository Stats
on:
  schedule:
    - cron: '0 0 * * *'
  push:
    branches:
      - main
  workflow_dispatch:

jobs:
  update-stats:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    permissions:
      contents: write
    steps:
      - name: Checkout code
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: Set up Python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v4
        with:
          python-version: '3.x'

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: pip install pyyaml requests

      - name: Fetch and Save Stats
        run: |
          python - <<EOF
          import requests
          import yaml
          import os

          repo_url = "https://api.github.com/repos/devicals/devicals.github.io"
          lang_url = f"{repo_url}/languages"

          # Fetch Repo Data
          repo_data = requests.get(repo_url).json()
          # Fetch Language Data
          lang_data = requests.get(lang_url).json()

          stats = {
              "stars": repo_data.get("stargazers_count", 0),
              "forks": repo_data.get("forks_count", 0),
              "watchers": repo_data.get("subscribers_count", 0),
              "size": repo_data.get("size", 0),
              "languages": []
          }

          total_bytes = sum(lang_data.values())
          if total_bytes > 0:
              for lang, bytes in lang_data.items():
                  percentage = round((bytes / total_bytes) * 100, 1)
                  stats["languages"].append({"name": lang, "percent": percentage})

          # Ensure directory exists
          os.makedirs('storage/internal', exist_ok=True)

          with open('storage/internal/stats.yaml', 'w') as f:
              yaml.dump(stats, f, default_flow_style=False)
          EOF

      - name: Commit and Push
        run: |
          git config --global user.name "github-actions[bot]"
          git config --global user.email "github-actions[bot]@users.noreply.github.com"
          git add storage/internal/stats.yaml
          git commit -m "Update repository statistics" || exit 0
          git push --force
---

      3. I have added back the fuctionality of using # to define where you want to be! Now you can add **#about**, **#blog**, or **#projects** at the end of the link to be on the Profile, Blog, or Projects tab respectively. Furthermore, blogs now had a numerical ID, displayed next to the date. With **#blog?id={ID}** where **{ID}** is the ID of the blog post, you can directly open to page to that post!
      4. Now practically everything are now defined using JSON, e.g. the blog posts, projects, even the books! This makes my life SO much easier making these posts and stuff, and makes my code just that tad bit cleaner and shorter! Hopefully because of this, I'll be making more blog posts now!
      5. As a Halloween special, I'm making a 3 chapter short psychological horror story that may release in a few weeks.
      6. Also, I've added back the [RSS feed](~/&id=8) feature!

      Anyways, that's all for now, have a very happy Halloween guys!

  - id: 9
    date: 12/03/2025
    title: "UI & Features Revamp"
    content: |-
      The entire website has now just been revamped! As you can see, everything looks more fresh and heck, more modern! I'll let you explore that on your own.

      Now onto the features!

      First of all, I added a contact me form on the main page, so you guys can send me emails from this very website! I also added a newsletter feed under it, you just plop your email there and BOOM!, you're subscribed!

      Secondly, the blog post "jump to tags" function has also been changed. As you can see above the big blog titles, there's a small line of text that contains the blog number and the blog date. The jump to tags now function using the blog number. The format is **#blog<#|-** with **<#|-** being the blog number. For example, to automatically jump to this blog post, you would go to **https://devicals.github.io/blogs#9**, note the main part: **#blog9**. Also, to view the latest blog post, you can now go to the tag **#blog0**!

      Alright, that's it for now, see y'all! (It has since been revamped again, twice!)

path: Website/storage/internal/pages/blogs.html
contents:
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Blogs - Error Dev</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=JetBrains+Mono:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="/storage/internal/styles/page-styles.css">
    <script src="/storage/internal/scripts/embed-detect.js"></script>
    <script src="/storage/internal/scripts/theme-manager.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/js-yaml/4.1.0/js-yaml.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/marked/11.1.1/marked.min.js"></script>
    <style>
        .blog-controls { position: fixed; top: 50px; right: 50px; z-index: 1000; background: hsla(var(--card), 0.8); backdrop-filter: blur(12px); border: 1px solid hsla(var(--primary), 0.2); padding: 10px 16px; box-shadow: 0 8px 32px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3); animation: floatIn 0.8s cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1) forwards; }
        @keyframes floatIn { from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(-20px); } to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); } }
        .blog-jump { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 10px; }
        .blog-jump label { font-size: 10px; font-weight: 700; text-transform: uppercase; letter-spacing: 1px; color: hsl(var(--primary)); }
        #blog-id-input { width: 50px; background: hsla(var(--background), 0.5); border: 1px solid hsl(var(--border)); color: hsl(var(--foreground)); padding: 4px 6px; font-family: 'JetBrains Mono', monospace; font-size: 13px; outline: none; }
        .blog-content { word-wrap: break-word; line-height: 1.6; }
        .blog-id { position: absolute; top: 24px; right: 24px; font-size: 12px; color: hsl(var(--muted-foreground)); font-weight: 600; }
        .blog-post { position: relative; }
        
        .shiki-container { background: #121212; border: 1px solid #2d2e2e; margin: 1.5rem 0; overflow: hidden; }
        .shiki-header { display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; padding: 0.6rem 1rem; background: #181818; border-bottom: 1px solid #2d2e2e; }
        .shiki-lang { color: #7e7e7e; font-size: 0.8rem; text-transform: uppercase; font-weight: 600; }
        .shiki-actions { display: flex; gap: 8px; }
        .shiki-btn { background: transparent; border: 1px solid #2d2e2e; color: #7e7e7e; padding: 4px 10px; font-size: 0.75rem; cursor: pointer; font-family: inherit; transition: all 0.2s ease; }
        .shiki-btn:hover { border-color: #dbd7ca; color: #dbd7ca; }
        .shiki-btn.active { border-color: #4d937b; color: #4d937b; }
        .shiki-container pre.shiki { margin: 0 !important; border: none !important; padding: 1rem !important; background-color: transparent !important; white-space: pre; overflow-x: auto; }
        .shiki-container.wrap-enabled pre.shiki { white-space: pre-wrap; word-break: break-all; }
        code.shiki-inline { background: #121212 !important; padding: 3px 6px !important; border: 1px solid #2d2e2e !important; font-family: 'JetBrains Mono', monospace !important; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; }
    </style>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="page-container">
        <h1 class="page-title">Blogs</h1>
        <div class="blog-controls" id="floating-jump-card">
            <div class="blog-jump">
                <label>Jump to</label>
                <input type="number" id="blog-id-input" placeholder="ID">
                <button onclick="window.jumpToBlog()" class="copy-btn" style="padding: 4px 10px;">Go</button>
                <button onclick="window.copyRSS()" class="copy-btn" id="rss-btn" style="padding: 4px 10px; background: transparent; border: 1px solid hsla(var(--primary), 0.5);">RSS URL</button>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="blog-posts" id="blog-posts"></div>
    </div>
    
    <script type="module">
        import { codeToHtml } from 'https://esm.sh/shiki@1.0.0';

        let blogsData = [];
        let isShikiWrapEnabled = localStorage.getItem('shikiWrapEnabled') !== 'false';

        marked.use({
            breaks: true, gfm: true, async: true,
            async walkTokens(token) {
                if (token.type === 'code') {
                    const shikiHtml = await codeToHtml(token.text, { lang: token.lang || 'text', theme: 'vitesse-dark' });
                    const header = `<div class="shiki-header"><span class="shiki-lang">${token.lang || 'text'}</span><div class="shiki-actions"><button class="shiki-btn wrap-btn">Wrap</button><button class="shiki-btn copy-btn">Copy</button></div></div>`;
                    token.type = 'html';
                    token.text = `<div class="shiki-container">${header}${shikiHtml}</div>`;
                } else if (token.type === 'codespan') {
                    const raw = await codeToHtml(token.text, { lang: 'text', theme: 'vitesse-dark' });
                    const inline = raw.replace(/<pre[^>]*>/, '').replace('</pre>', '').replace('<code', '<code class="shiki-inline"');
                    token.type = 'html';
                    token.text = inline;
                }
            }
        });

        async function loadYAML(path) {
            const response = await fetch(path);
            const text = await response.text();
            return jsyaml.load(text);
        }

        function parseDate(dateStr) {
            const [day, month, year] = dateStr.split('/').map(Number);
            return new Date(year, month - 1, day);
        }

        async function renderBlogs(blogs) {
            const container = document.getElementById('blog-posts');
            container.innerHTML = '';
            for (const blog of blogs) {
                const blogPost = document.createElement('div');
                blogPost.className = 'blog-post';
                blogPost.id = `blog-${blog.id}`;
                const htmlContent = await marked.parse(blog.content);
                blogPost.innerHTML = `<div class="blog-id">#${blog.id}</div><div class="blog-header"><a href="#" class="blog-title" onclick="window.copyBlogLink(event, ${blog.id})">${blog.title}</a><div class="blog-date">${blog.date}</div></div><div class="blog-content">${htmlContent}</div>`;
                container.appendChild(blogPost);
            }
            setupShikiInteractions();
        }

        function setupShikiInteractions() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.shiki-container').forEach(container => {
                const wrapBtn = container.querySelector('.wrap-btn');
                if (isShikiWrapEnabled) {
                    container.classList.add('wrap-enabled');
                    if (wrapBtn) { wrapBtn.classList.add('active'); wrapBtn.textContent = 'Wrap: On'; }
                } else {
                    if (wrapBtn) wrapBtn.textContent = 'Wrap: Off';
                }
            });
        }

        function scrollToBlogId(id) {
            const el = document.getElementById(`blog-${id}`);
            if (el) {
                el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                el.style.borderColor = 'hsl(var(--accent))';
                setTimeout(() => el.style.borderColor = 'hsl(var(--border))', 2000);
            } else {
                alert(`Blog #${id} not found.`);
            }
        }

        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.matches('.shiki-btn.copy-btn')) {
                const container = e.target.closest('.shiki-container');
                const codeBlock = container?.querySelector('pre.shiki code');
                if (codeBlock) {
                    navigator.clipboard.writeText(codeBlock.innerText).then(() => {
                        e.target.textContent = 'Copied!';
                        setTimeout(() => e.target.textContent = 'Copy', 2000);
                    });
                }
            }
            if (e.target.matches('.shiki-btn.wrap-btn')) {
                isShikiWrapEnabled = !isShikiWrapEnabled;
                localStorage.setItem('shikiWrapEnabled', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                document.querySelectorAll('.shiki-container').forEach(container => {
                    const wrapBtn = container.querySelector('.wrap-btn');
                    container.classList.toggle('wrap-enabled', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                    if (wrapBtn) {
                        wrapBtn.classList.toggle('active', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                        wrapBtn.textContent = isShikiWrapEnabled ? 'Wrap: On' : 'Wrap: Off';
                    }
                });
            }

            const link = e.target.closest('a');
            if (link) {
                const href = link.getAttribute('href');
                if (!href) return;

                if (href.match(/^~\/&id=(\d+)$/)) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const id = href.split('=')[1];
                    scrollToBlogId(id);
                    return;
                }

                if (href.startsWith('./#')) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const hash = href.substring(2); 
                    window.parent.location.hash = hash;
                    return;
                }
            }
        });

        window.copyBlogLink = (e, id) => { e.preventDefault(); const url = `https://devicals.github.io/#page=blogs&id=${id}`; navigator.clipboard.writeText(url).then(() => { e.target.textContent = "Link Copied!"; setTimeout(() => e.target.textContent = blogsData.find(b=>b.id===id).title, 2000); }); document.getElementById(`blog-${id}`).scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }); };
        window.jumpToBlog = () => { 
            const id = document.getElementById('blog-id-input').value; 
            if (!id) return; 
            scrollToBlogId(id);
        };
        window.copyRSS = () => { const url = "https://github.com/devicals/devicals.github.io/raw/refs/heads/main/storage/internal/blogs.xml"; navigator.clipboard.writeText(url).then(() => { const btn = document.getElementById('rss-btn'); btn.textContent = 'Copied!'; setTimeout(() => { btn.textContent = 'RSS URL'; }, 2000); }); };

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
            try {
                const data = await loadYAML('/storage/data/blogs.yaml');
                if (!data || !data.blogs) return;
                blogsData = data.blogs.sort((a, b) => parseDate(b.date) - parseDate(a.date));
                await renderBlogs(blogsData);
                const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.hash.substring(1));
                const id = params.get('id');
                if (id) setTimeout(() => { const el = document.getElementById(`blog-${id}`); if (el) el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }); }, 500);
            } catch (error) { console.error(error); }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <style>

<body>
    <div class="page-container">
        <h1 class="page-title" id="page-title">Loading...</h1>
        <div id="breadcrumb" class="breadcrumb">
            <div class="breadcrumb-path" id="breadcrumb-path"></div>
            <div class="breadcrumb-nav">
                <button class="breadcrumb-btn" id="prev-btn" disabled>â† Prev</button>
                <button class="breadcrumb-btn" id="next-btn" disabled>Next â†’</button>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div id="content"></div>
        <button class="scroll-to-top" id="scroll-to-top">â†‘ Top</button>

    <script type="module">
        import { codeToHtml } from 'https://esm.sh/shiki@1.0.0';

        let currentPath = [];
        let pagesData = [];
        let customPageData = null;
        let rootPageId = null;
        let isShikiWrapEnabled = localStorage.getItem('shikiWrapEnabled') !== 'false';

        marked.use({
            breaks: true, gfm: true, async: true,
            async walkTokens(token) {
                if (token.type === 'code') {
                    const shikiHtml = await codeToHtml(token.text, { lang: token.lang || 'text', theme: 'vitesse-dark' });
                    const header = `<div class="shiki-header"><span class="shiki-lang">${token.lang || 'text'}</span><div class="shiki-actions"><button class="shiki-btn wrap-btn">Wrap</button><button class="shiki-btn copy-btn">Copy</button></div></div>`;
                    token.type = 'html';
                    token.text = `<div class="shiki-container">${header}${shikiHtml}</div>`;
                } else if (token.type === 'codespan') {
                    const raw = await codeToHtml(token.text, { lang: 'text', theme: 'vitesse-dark' });
                    const inline = raw.replace(/<pre[^>]*>/, '').replace('</pre>', '').replace('<code', '<code class="shiki-inline"');
                    token.type = 'html';
                    token.text = inline;
                }
            }
        });

        async function loadYAML(path) {
            try {
                const resp = await fetch(path);
                if (!resp.ok) return null;
                const text = await resp.text();
                return jsyaml.load(text);
            } catch (e) { return null; }
        }

        function getParentParams() { return new URLSearchParams(window.parent.location.hash.substring(1)); }
        function buildNavURL(path) {
            if (path.length === 0) return `#page=${rootPageId}`;
            return `#page=${rootPageId}&nav=${path.map(p => p.id).join('>')}`;
        }

        function updateBreadcrumb() {
            const container = document.getElementById('breadcrumb-path');
            if (!customPageData) return;
            let html = `<a href="${buildNavURL([])}" onclick="window.navigateTo([]); return false;">${customPageData.name || 'Root'}</a>`;
            currentPath.forEach((item, i) => {
                const url = buildNavURL(currentPath.slice(0, i + 1));
                html += `<span>/</span><a href="${url}" onclick='window.navigateTo(${JSON.stringify(currentPath.slice(0, i + 1))}); return false;'>${item.name}</a>`;
            });
            container.innerHTML = html;
        }

        window.navigateTo = async function(path) {
            currentPath = path;
            updateBreadcrumb();
            window.parent.history.replaceState(null, null, buildNavURL(path));

            let siblingYaml = customPageData.path;
            if (path.length > 0) {
                const lastItem = path[path.length - 1];
                if (lastItem.type === 'section') siblingYaml = lastItem.path;
                else if (path.length > 1) siblingYaml = path[path.length - 2].path;
            }

            const dirData = await loadYAML('/storage/data/' + siblingYaml);
            pagesData = dirData ? dirData.pages : [];

            const content = document.getElementById('content');
            if (path.length === 0) {
                await renderSections(customPageData.path);
            } else {
                const item = path[path.length - 1];
                if (item.type === 'section') {
                    await renderSections(item.path);
                } else if (item.type === 'md') {
                    const resp = await fetch('/storage/data/' + item.path);
                    const md = await resp.text();
                    content.innerHTML = `<div class="md-content">${await marked.parse(md)}</div>`;
                    setupShikiInteractions();
                } else if (item.type === 'raw') {
                    const resp = await fetch('/storage/data/' + item.path);
                    const raw = await resp.text();
                    content.innerHTML = `<pre style="background:#121212;padding:20px;border:1px solid #2d2e2e;color:#dbd7ca;white-space:pre-wrap;">${raw.replace(/</g, "&lt;")}</pre>`;
                }
            }
            updateNavButtons();
        };

        function updateNavButtons() {
            const prevBtn = document.getElementById('prev-btn');
            const nextBtn = document.getElementById('next-btn');
            if (currentPath.length === 0 || !pagesData.length) { prevBtn.disabled = nextBtn.disabled = true; return; }
            const item = currentPath[currentPath.length - 1];
            const idx = pagesData.findIndex(p => String(p.id) === String(item.id));
            if (idx === -1) { prevBtn.disabled = nextBtn.disabled = true; return; }
            const basePath = item.path.substring(0, item.path.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);
            const setBtn = (btn, targetIdx) => {
                btn.disabled = targetIdx < 0 || targetIdx >= pagesData.length;
                btn.onclick = btn.disabled ? null : () => {
                    const p = pagesData[targetIdx];
                    const type = (typeof p.type === 'object' ? p.type.type : p.type) || (p.path.endsWith('.yaml') ? 'section' : 'md');
                    window.navigateTo([...currentPath.slice(0, -1), { id: String(p.id), name: p.name, path: basePath + p.path, type }]);
                };
            };
            setBtn(prevBtn, idx - 1);
            setBtn(nextBtn, idx + 1);
        }

        async function parseURLNav() {
            const params = getParentParams();
            let nav = params.get('nav') || "";
            nav = decodeURIComponent(nav).replace(/,/g, '>');
            if (!nav) return [];
            const ids = nav.split('>').filter(x => x);
            const path = [];
            let curYaml = customPageData.path;
            for (const id of ids) {
                const data = await loadYAML('/storage/data/' + curYaml);
                if (!data || !data.pages) break;
                const p = data.pages.find(x => String(x.id) === id);
                if (!p) break;
                const base = curYaml.substring(0, curYaml.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);
                const full = base + p.path;
                const type = (typeof p.type === 'object' ? p.type.type : p.type) || (p.path.endsWith('.yaml') ? 'section' : 'md');
                path.push({ id: String(p.id), name: p.name, path: full, type });
                if (type === 'section') curYaml = full;
            }
            return path;
        }

        async function renderSections(yaml) {
            const data = await loadYAML('/storage/data/' + yaml);
            if (!data) return;
            const base = yaml.substring(0, yaml.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);
            const grid = document.createElement('div');
            grid.className = 'section-grid';
            data.pages.forEach(p => {
                const card = document.createElement('a');
                card.className = 'section-card';
                card.onclick = (e) => {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    const type = (typeof p.type === 'object' ? p.type.type : p.type) || (p.path.endsWith('.yaml') ? 'section' : 'md');
                    window.navigateTo([...currentPath, { id: String(p.id), name: p.name, path: base + p.path, type }]);
                };
                card.innerHTML = `<div class="section-card-title">${p.name}</div><div class="section-card-type">${(typeof p.type === 'object' ? p.type.type : (p.type || 'SECTION')).toUpperCase()}</div>`;
                grid.appendChild(card);
            });
            document.getElementById('content').innerHTML = '';
            document.getElementById('content').appendChild(grid);
        }

        function setupShikiInteractions() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.shiki-container').forEach(container => {
                const wrapBtn = container.querySelector('.wrap-btn');
                if (isShikiWrapEnabled) {
                    container.classList.add('wrap-enabled');
                    if (wrapBtn) { wrapBtn.classList.add('active'); wrapBtn.textContent = 'Wrap: On'; }
                } else {
                    if (wrapBtn) wrapBtn.textContent = 'Wrap: Off';
                }
            });
        }

        async function init() {
            rootPageId = getParentParams().get('page');
            const custom = await loadYAML('/storage/data/custom.yaml');
            if (!custom || !custom.customPages) return;
            for (const key in custom.customPages) {
                const category = custom.customPages[key];
                if (category.sub && Array.isArray(category.sub)) {
                    const found = category.sub.find(p => p.id === rootPageId);
                    if (found) { customPageData = found; break; }
                }
            }
            if (!customPageData) return;
            document.getElementById('page-title').textContent = customPageData.name;
            await window.navigateTo(await parseURLNav());
        }
        
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.matches('.shiki-btn.copy-btn')) {
                const container = e.target.closest('.shiki-container');
                const codeBlock = container?.querySelector('pre.shiki code');
                if (codeBlock) navigator.clipboard.writeText(codeBlock.innerText).then(() => { e.target.textContent = 'Copied!'; setTimeout(() => e.target.textContent = 'Copy', 2000); });
            }
            if (e.target.matches('.shiki-btn.wrap-btn')) {
                isShikiWrapEnabled = !isShikiWrapEnabled;
                localStorage.setItem('shikiWrapEnabled', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                document.querySelectorAll('.shiki-container').forEach(container => {
                    const wrapBtn = container.querySelector('.wrap-btn');
                    container.classList.toggle('wrap-enabled', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                    if (wrapBtn) { wrapBtn.classList.toggle('active', isShikiWrapEnabled); wrapBtn.textContent = isShikiWrapEnabled ? 'Wrap: On' : 'Wrap: Off'; }
                });
            }
        });

        window.addEventListener('scroll', () => document.getElementById('scroll-to-top').classList.toggle('visible', window.scrollY > 300));
        document.getElementById('scroll-to-top').onclick = () => window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
        window.addEventListener('hashchange', async () => await window.navigateTo(await parseURLNav()));
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>

    <div id="copy-toast">LINK COPIED TO CLIPBOARD</div>
    
    <div class="page-container">
        <h1 class="page-title">Downloads</h1>
        
        <div class="downloads-list" id="downloads-list"></div>
    </div>
    
    <script>
        async function loadYAML(path) {
            const response = await fetch(path);
            const text = await response.text();
            return jsyaml.load(text);
        }

        function copyLink(id) {
            const baseUrl = window.parent.location.origin + window.parent.location.pathname;
            const newHash = `page=downloads&id=${id}`;
            const fullUrl = `${baseUrl}#${newHash}`;
            
            window.parent.history.replaceState(null, null, `#${newHash}`);
            
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(fullUrl).then(() => {
                const toast = document.getElementById('copy-toast');
                toast.textContent = `LINK COPIED [#${id}]`;
                toast.style.display = 'block';
                setTimeout(() => { toast.style.display = 'none'; }, 2000);
            });

            document.querySelectorAll('.download-card').forEach(card => card.style.borderColor = '');
            
            const activeCard = document.getElementById(`download-${id}`);
            if (activeCard) {
                activeCard.style.borderColor = 'hsl(var(--accent))';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    activeCard.style.borderColor = ''; 
                }, 1000);
            }
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
            try {
                const data = await loadYAML('/storage/data/downloads.yaml');
                
                if (!data || !data.downloads) {
                    console.error('No downloads data found');
                    return;
                }
                
                const container = document.getElementById('downloads-list');
                
                data.downloads.forEach((download) => {
                    const card = document.createElement('div');
                    card.className = 'download-card';
                    card.id = `download-${download.id}`;
                    
                    const header = document.createElement('div');
                    header.className = 'download-header';
                    
                    const leftGroup = document.createElement('div');
                    leftGroup.className = 'download-left';
                    leftGroup.title = 'Click to copy link';
                    leftGroup.onclick = () => copyLink(download.id);

                    const idSpan = document.createElement('span');
                    idSpan.className = 'download-id';
                    idSpan.textContent = `#${download.id}`;

                    const name = document.createElement('span');
                    name.className = 'download-name';
                    name.textContent = download.name;
                    
                    leftGroup.appendChild(idSpan);
                    leftGroup.appendChild(name);

                    const btn = document.createElement('a');
                    btn.className = 'download-btn';
                    btn.href = download.url;
                    btn.target = '_blank';
                    btn.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
                    btn.textContent = 'Download';
                    
                    header.appendChild(leftGroup);
                    header.appendChild(btn);
                    
                    const description = document.createElement('div');
                    description.className = 'download-description';
                    description.textContent = download.description;
                    
                    card.appendChild(header);
                    card.appendChild(description);
                    container.appendChild(card);
                });

                const handleHash = () => {
                    const hash = window.location.hash.substring(1);
                    const params = new URLSearchParams(hash);
                    const id = params.get('id');

                    if (id) {
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            const element = document.getElementById(`download-${id}`);
                            if (element) {
                                element.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                                element.style.borderColor = 'hsl(var(--accent))';
                                setTimeout(() => {
                                    element.style.borderColor = ''; 
                                }, 1000);
                            }
                        }, 300);
                    }
                };

                handleHash();

            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error loading downloads:', error);
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        function loadGiscus() {
            const script = document.createElement('script');
            script.src = "https://giscus.app/client.js";
            script.setAttribute('data-repo', "devicals/devicals.github.io");
            script.setAttribute('data-repo-id', "R_kgDOOHsfMg");
            script.setAttribute('data-category', "General");
            script.setAttribute('data-category-id', "DIC_kwDOOHsfMs4C0rjJ");
            script.setAttribute('data-mapping', "pathname");
            script.setAttribute('data-strict', "0");
            script.setAttribute('data-reactions-enabled', "0");
            script.setAttribute('data-emit-metadata', "0");
            script.setAttribute('data-input-position', "top");
            script.setAttribute('data-lang', "en");
            script.setAttribute('crossorigin', "anonymous");
            script.async = true;

            script.setAttribute('data-theme', 'noborder_dark');

            document.getElementById('giscus-slot').appendChild(script);
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            setTimeout(loadGiscus, 100);
        });

        function copyTemplate() {
            const template = `Rating: <Your Rating>/5 stars
Feedback: <Your Feedback>`;
            
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(template).then(() => {
                const btn = event.target;
                const originalText = btn.textContent;
                btn.textContent = 'Copied!';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    btn.textContent = originalText;
                }, 2000);
            });
        }
    </script>

<body>
    <div id="copy-toast">LINK COPIED TO CLIPBOARD</div>
    <div class="page-container">
        <h1 class="page-title" id="gallery-title">Gallery</h1>
        
        <div class="filter-box" id="filter-box">
            <div class="filter-toggle" id="filter-toggle" onclick="toggleFilter()">&lt;</div>
            <span class="filter-label">GALLERY FILTER</span>
            
            <label id="label-img" style="display:none">
                <input type="checkbox" id="filter-img" checked onchange="applyFilters()"> IMAGES
            </label>
            <label id="label-video" style="display:none">
                <input type="checkbox" id="filter-video" checked onchange="applyFilters()"> VIDEOS
            </label>
            <label id="label-audio" style="display:none">
                <input type="checkbox" id="filter-audio" checked onchange="applyFilters()"> AUDIO
            </label>

            <div class="jump-container">
                <span class="filter-label">JUMP TO ID</span>
                <input type="number" id="jump-id-input" class="jump-input" placeholder="ID #">
                <button class="jump-btn" onclick="executeJump()">Jump</button>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="gallery-grid" id="gallery-grid"></div>
    </div>
    
    <script>
        let galleryData = [];
        let imgExtensions = [];
        let videoExtensions = [];
        let audioExtensions = [];
        let galleryType = 'gallery';
        let currentPageId = '';
        let yamlBaseDir = "";

        async function parseExtensionList(path) {
            try {
                const resp = await fetch(path);
                if (!resp.ok) return [];
                const text = await resp.text();
                const regex = /\(([\s\S]*?)\)/;
                const match = text.match(regex);
                if (!match) return [];
                return match[1].split(/[,\n]/).map(s => s.trim().replace(/["']/g, '')).filter(s => s.length > 0);
            } catch (e) { return []; }
        }

        function getItemType(filename) {
            if (!filename) return 'NONE';
            const ext = filename.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            if (imgExtensions.includes(ext)) return 'IMAGE';
            if (videoExtensions.includes(ext)) return 'VIDEO';
            if (audioExtensions.includes(ext)) return 'AUDIO';
            return 'UNKNOWN';
        }

        async function loadGallery() {
            const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            const filePath = params.get('file');
            galleryType = params.get('type') || 'gallery';
            const parentHash = window.parent.location.hash.substring(1);
            const parentParams = new URLSearchParams(parentHash);
            currentPageId = parentParams.get('page') || 'home';

            if (!filePath) return;

            if (filePath.includes('/')) {
                yamlBaseDir = filePath.substring(0, filePath.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);
            } else {
                yamlBaseDir = "";
            }

            [imgExtensions, videoExtensions, audioExtensions] = await Promise.all([
                parseExtensionList('/storage/internal/ext/image.list'),
                parseExtensionList('/storage/internal/ext/video.list'),
                parseExtensionList('/storage/internal/ext/music.list')
            ]);

            const response = await fetch('/storage/data/' + filePath);
            const text = await response.text();
            const data = jsyaml.load(text);
            galleryData = data.items || [];

            renderGallery();
            const jumpId = params.get('id');
            if (jumpId) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    const el = document.getElementById(`item-${jumpId}`);
                    if (el) el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                }, 800);
            }
        }

        function copyLink(id) {
            const newHash = `page=${currentPageId}&id=${id}`;
            const baseUrl = window.parent.location.origin + window.parent.location.pathname;
            const fullUrl = `${baseUrl}#${newHash}`;
            window.parent.history.replaceState(null, null, `#${newHash}`);
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(fullUrl).then(() => {
                const toast = document.getElementById('copy-toast');
                toast.textContent = `LINK COPIED & URL UPDATED [#${id}]`;
                toast.style.display = 'block';
                setTimeout(() => { toast.style.display = 'none'; }, 2000);
            });
            document.querySelectorAll('.gallery-card').forEach(card => card.style.borderColor = '#2d2e2e');
            const activeCard = document.getElementById(`item-${id}`);
            if (activeCard) activeCard.style.borderColor = 'hsl(var(--accent))';
        }

        function executeJump() {
            const id = document.getElementById('jump-id-input').value;
            const el = document.getElementById(`item-${id}`);
            if (el) {
                el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                el.style.outline = '2px solid hsl(var(--accent))';
                setTimeout(() => el.style.outline = 'none', 2000);
            }
        }

        function renderGallery() {
            const container = document.getElementById('gallery-grid');
            container.innerHTML = '';
            
            const showImgs = document.getElementById('filter-img').checked;
            const showVideos = document.getElementById('filter-video').checked;
            const showAudio = document.getElementById('filter-audio').checked;

            let typesFound = { IMAGE: false, VIDEO: false, AUDIO: false };
            const headerItem = galleryData.find(i => i.id === 0);
            if (headerItem) {
                const headCard = document.createElement('div');
                headCard.className = 'gallery-card body-only';
                headCard.id = `item-0`;
                headCard.innerHTML = headerItem.body ? marked.parse(headerItem.body) : '';
                container.appendChild(headCard);
            }

            galleryData.forEach((item, index) => {
                if (item.id === 0) return;

                const id = item.id || index;
                const type = getItemType(item.path);
                const resolvedPath = `/storage/data/${yamlBaseDir}${item.path}`;

                if (type !== 'UNKNOWN') typesFound[type] = true;
                if (galleryType === 'gallery.img' && type !== 'IMAGE') return;
                if (galleryType === 'gallery.video' && type !== 'VIDEO') return;
                if (galleryType === 'gallery.audio' && type !== 'AUDIO') return;
                
                if (galleryType === 'gallery') {
                    if (type === 'IMAGE' && !showImgs) return;
                    if (type === 'VIDEO' && !showVideos) return;
                    if (type === 'AUDIO' && !showAudio) return;
                }

                const card = document.createElement('div');
                card.className = 'gallery-card';
                card.id = `item-${id}`;
                
                let mediaHtml = '';
                if (type === 'IMAGE') {
                    mediaHtml = `<img src="${resolvedPath}" loading="lazy">`;
                } else if (type === 'VIDEO') {
                    mediaHtml = `<video src="${resolvedPath}" controls preload="metadata"></video>`;
                } else if (type === 'AUDIO') {
                    mediaHtml = `
                        <div class="audio-ui">
                            <div class="audio-error-msg" id="error-${index}"><strong>Cannot find specified audio file.</strong></div>
                            <audio id="aud-${index}" src="${resolvedPath}" preload="metadata"></audio>
                            <div class="audio-controls-row">
                                <button class="audio-btn" id="play-btn-${index}">â–¶</button>
                                <input type="range" id="seek-${index}" class="audio-progress" value="0" step="0.1" max="100">
                                <button class="audio-btn audio-btn-small" id="repeat-btn-${index}" title="Repeat Once">1</button>
                                <button class="audio-btn audio-btn-small" id="loop-btn-${index}" title="Loop">âˆ</button>
                            </div>
                            <div class="audio-time-display" id="time-${index}">00:00 / 00:00</div>
                        </div>`;
                }

                card.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="gallery-header">
                        <div class="header-left" onclick="copyLink('${id}')" title="Click to copy link">
                            <span class="gallery-id-label">#${id}</span>
                            <span class="gallery-type-label">${type}</span>
                        </div>
                        <a href="${resolvedPath}" download class="download-btn">Download</a>
                    </div>
                    <div class="gallery-media-container">
                        ${mediaHtml}
                    </div>
                    ${item.title ? `
                    <div class="gallery-info">
                        <div class="gallery-item-title" onclick="copyLink('${id}')">${item.title}</div>
                        ${item.description ? `<div class="gallery-item-desc">${item.description}</div>` : ''}
                    </div>` : ''}
                `;
                container.appendChild(card);

                if (type === 'AUDIO') setupAudioPlayer(index);
            });
            document.getElementById('label-img').style.display = typesFound.IMAGE ? 'flex' : 'none';
            document.getElementById('label-video').style.display = typesFound.VIDEO ? 'flex' : 'none';
            document.getElementById('label-audio').style.display = typesFound.AUDIO ? 'flex' : 'none';
        }

        function setupAudioPlayer(index) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                const aud = document.getElementById(`aud-${index}`);
                const playBtn = document.getElementById(`play-btn-${index}`);
                const seek = document.getElementById(`seek-${index}`);
                const timeDisplay = document.getElementById(`time-${index}`);
                const repeatBtn = document.getElementById(`repeat-btn-${index}`);
                const loopBtn = document.getElementById(`loop-btn-${index}`);
                const errorDisplay = document.getElementById(`error-${index}`);
                let repeatOnce = false;
                
                const formatTime = (s) => isNaN(s) || s === Infinity ? '00:00' : `${Math.floor(s/60).toString().padStart(2,'0')}:${Math.floor(s%60).toString().padStart(2,'0')}`;
                
                if (!aud || !playBtn) return;

                const disablePlayer = () => {
                    playBtn.disabled = true;
                    seek.disabled = true;
                    repeatBtn.disabled = true;
                    loopBtn.disabled = true;
                    errorDisplay.style.display = 'block';
                    timeDisplay.textContent = "00:00 / 00:00";
                };

                aud.addEventListener('error', disablePlayer);

                aud.addEventListener('loadedmetadata', () => {
                    if (aud.duration === 0 || isNaN(aud.duration)) {
                        disablePlayer();
                    } else {
                        seek.max = aud.duration;
                        timeDisplay.textContent = `00:00 / ${formatTime(aud.duration)}`;
                    }
                });
                
                playBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    if (aud.paused) { aud.play(); playBtn.innerHTML = 'â¸'; }
                    else { aud.pause(); playBtn.innerHTML = 'â–¶'; }
                });
                
                repeatBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    repeatOnce = !repeatOnce;
                    repeatBtn.classList.toggle('active', repeatOnce);
                    if (repeatOnce) { aud.loop = false; loopBtn.classList.remove('active'); }
                });
                
                loopBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    aud.loop = !aud.loop;
                    loopBtn.classList.toggle('active', aud.loop);
                    if (aud.loop) { repeatOnce = false; repeatBtn.classList.remove('active'); }
                });
                
                aud.addEventListener('timeupdate', () => {
                    seek.value = aud.currentTime;
                    timeDisplay.textContent = `${formatTime(aud.currentTime)} / ${formatTime(aud.duration)}`;
                });
                
                seek.addEventListener('input', () => { aud.currentTime = parseFloat(seek.value); });
                
                aud.addEventListener('ended', () => {
                    if (repeatOnce) {
                        aud.currentTime = 0; aud.play();
                        repeatOnce = false; repeatBtn.classList.remove('active');
                    } else { playBtn.innerHTML = 'â–¶'; }
                });
            }, 0);
        }

        function applyFilters() { renderGallery(); }

        function toggleFilter() {
            const filterBox = document.getElementById('filter-box');
            const toggle = document.getElementById('filter-toggle');
            filterBox.classList.toggle('collapsed');
            toggle.innerHTML = filterBox.classList.contains('collapsed') ? '&gt;' : '&lt;';
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', loadGallery);
        document.getElementById('jump-id-input')?.addEventListener('keypress', (e) => {
            if (e.key === 'Enter') executeJump();
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        function loadGiscus() {
            const script = document.createElement('script');
            script.src = "https://giscus.app/client.js";
            script.setAttribute('data-repo', "devicals/devicals.github.io");
            script.setAttribute('data-repo-id', "R_kgDOOHsfMg");
            script.setAttribute('data-category', "Guestbook");
            script.setAttribute('data-category-id', "DIC_kwDOOHsfMs4C1JOq");
            script.setAttribute('data-mapping', "pathname");
            script.setAttribute('data-strict', "0");
            script.setAttribute('data-reactions-enabled', "0");
            script.setAttribute('data-emit-metadata', "0");
            script.setAttribute('data-input-position', "top");
            script.setAttribute('data-lang', "en");
            script.setAttribute('crossorigin', "anonymous");
            script.async = true;

            script.setAttribute('data-theme', 'noborder_dark');

            document.getElementById('giscus-slot').appendChild(script);
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
            setTimeout(loadGiscus, 100);
        });
    </script>

    <script>
        async function loadYAML(path) {
            const response = await fetch(path);
            const text = await response.text();
            return jsyaml.load(text);
        }

        function parseDate(dateStr) {
            const [day, month, year] = dateStr.split('/').map(Number);
            return new Date(year, month - 1, day);
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
            try {
                const data = await loadYAML('/storage/data/home.yaml');
                const homeData = data.home;
                
                if (homeData.bio) {
                    const bioCard = document.querySelector('.bio-card');
                    bioCard.innerHTML = marked.parse(homeData.bio);
                }
                
                if (homeData.skills) {
                    const skillsGrid = document.querySelector('.skills-grid');
                    homeData.skills.forEach(skillItem => {
                        const skillText = typeof skillItem === 'string' ? skillItem : skillItem.skill;
                        const skillLink = typeof skillItem === 'object' ? skillItem.link : null;
                        
                        if (skillLink) {
                            const card = document.createElement('a');
                            card.className = 'skill-card skill-card-link';
                            card.href = skillLink;
                            card.target = '_blank';
                            card.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
                            card.textContent = skillText;
                            skillsGrid.appendChild(card);
                        } else {
                            const card = document.createElement('div');
                            card.className = 'skill-card';
                            card.textContent = skillText;
                            skillsGrid.appendChild(card);
                        }
                    });
                }
                
                if (homeData.socials) {
                    const socialsGrid = document.querySelector('.socials-grid');
                    homeData.socials.forEach(social => {
                        const card = document.createElement('a');
                        card.className = 'social-card';
                        card.href = social.link;
                        card.target = '_blank';
                        card.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
                        card.textContent = social.name;
                        socialsGrid.appendChild(card);
                    });
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error loading home page:', error);
            }

            try {
                const blogData = await loadYAML('/storage/data/blogs.yaml');
                if (blogData && blogData.blogs && blogData.blogs.length > 0) {
                    const sortedBlogs = blogData.blogs.sort((a, b) => parseDate(b.date) - parseDate(a.date));
                    const latest = sortedBlogs[0];

                    const tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
                    tempDiv.innerHTML = marked.parse(latest.content);
                    const plainText = tempDiv.textContent || tempDiv.innerText || "";

                    let excerpt = plainText.trim();
                    if (excerpt.length > 100) {
                        excerpt = excerpt.substring(0, 100).replace(/[ ,.]*$/, "") + "...";
                    }

                    const container = document.getElementById('blog-preview-container');
                    
                    container.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="card blog-preview-card" style="cursor: pointer;" onclick="window.parent.location.hash = 'page=blogs'; window.parent.loadPage('blogs');">
                            <div class="preview-title">${latest.title}</div>
                            <div class="preview-date">${latest.date}</div>
                            <div class="preview-excerpt">${excerpt}</div>
                        </div>
                    `;
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error loading latest blog:', error);
            }
            
            if (window.location.hash) {
                const hash = window.location.hash.substring(1);
                const target = document.getElementById(hash);
                if (target) {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
                    }, 100);
                }
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
            const renderStats = (data) => {
                if (!data) return;
                document.getElementById('stars').textContent = (data.stars ?? 0).toLocaleString();
                document.getElementById('forks').textContent = (data.forks ?? 0).toLocaleString();
                document.getElementById('watchers').textContent = (data.watchers ?? 0).toLocaleString();
                document.getElementById('size').textContent = (data.size ?? 0).toLocaleString();

                const container = document.getElementById('languages-container');
                container.innerHTML = '';

                if (data.languages) {
                    data.languages.forEach(lang => {
                        const langItem = document.createElement('div');
                        langItem.className = 'language-item';
                        langItem.innerHTML = `
                            <div class="language-header">
                                <span class="language-name">${lang.name}</span>
                                <span class="language-percent">${lang.percent}%</span>
                            </div>
                            <div class="language-bar"><div class="language-fill" style="width: 0%"></div></div>
                        `;
                        container.appendChild(langItem);
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            const fill = langItem.querySelector('.language-fill');
                            if (fill) fill.style.width = `${lang.percent}%`;
                        }, 100);
                    });
                }
            };

            try {
                const response = await fetch('/storage/internal/stats.yaml');
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error("File not found");
                
                const yamlText = await response.text();
                const stats = jsyaml.load(yamlText);
                
                if (!stats || stats.stars === undefined) throw new Error("Incomplete YAML");
                
                console.log("Loaded from YAML successfully");
                renderStats(stats);

            } catch (e) {
                console.warn("Local YAML failed, falling back to Live API...", e);
                try {
                    const repoRes = await fetch('https://api.github.com/repos/devicals/devicals.github.io');
                    const repoData = await repoRes.json();
                    const langRes = await fetch('https://api.github.com/repos/devicals/devicals.github.io/languages');
                    const langData = await langRes.json();

                    const total = Object.values(langData).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
                    const fallbackData = {
                        stars: repoData.stargazers_count,
                        forks: repoData.forks_count,
                        watchers: repoData.subscribers_count,
                        size: repoData.size,
                        languages: Object.entries(langData).map(([name, bytes]) => ({
                            name,
                            percent: ((bytes / total) * 100).toFixed(1)
                        }))
                    };
                    renderStats(fallbackData);
                } catch (err) {
                    ['stars', 'forks', 'watchers', 'size'].forEach(id => {
                        document.getElementById(id).textContent = 'Error';
                    });
                }
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">

        .md-content { word-wrap: break-word; overflow-wrap: break-word; word-break: break-word; max-width: 100%; overflow-x: hidden; }
        .md-content img { max-width: 100%; height: auto; }
        .md-content p, .md-content li, .md-content span { white-space: normal; }
        
        .shiki-container { background: #121212; border: 1px solid #2d2e2e; margin: 1.5rem 0; overflow: hidden; }
        .shiki-header { display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; padding: 0.6rem 1rem; background: #181818; border-bottom: 1px solid #2d2e2e; }
        .shiki-lang { color: #7e7e7e; font-size: 0.8rem; text-transform: uppercase; font-weight: 600; }
        .shiki-actions { display: flex; gap: 8px; }
        .shiki-btn { background: transparent; border: 1px solid #2d2e2e; color: #7e7e7e; padding: 4px 10px; font-size: 0.75rem; cursor: pointer; font-family: inherit; transition: all 0.2s ease; }
        .shiki-btn:hover { border-color: #dbd7ca; color: #dbd7ca; }
        .shiki-btn.active { border-color: #4d937b; color: #4d937b; }
        .shiki-container pre.shiki { margin: 0 !important; border: none !important; padding: 1rem !important; background-color: transparent !important; white-space: pre; overflow-x: auto; }
        .shiki-container.wrap-enabled pre.shiki { white-space: pre-wrap; word-break: break-all; }
        code.shiki-inline { background: #121212 !important; padding: 3px 6px !important; border: 1px solid #2d2e2e !important; font-family: 'JetBrains Mono', monospace !important; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; }
    </style>

<body>
    <div class="page-container">
        <div class="card bio-card">
            <div class="md-content" id="md-content"></div>
        </div>
    </div>
    
    <script type="module">
        import { codeToHtml } from 'https://esm.sh/shiki@1.0.0';
        
        let isShikiWrapEnabled = localStorage.getItem('shikiWrapEnabled') !== 'false';

        marked.use({
            breaks: true, gfm: true, async: true,
            async walkTokens(token) {
                if (token.type === 'code') {
                    const shikiHtml = await codeToHtml(token.text, { lang: token.lang || 'text', theme: 'vitesse-dark' });
                    const header = `<div class="shiki-header"><span class="shiki-lang">${token.lang || 'text'}</span><div class="shiki-actions"><button class="shiki-btn wrap-btn">Wrap</button><button class="shiki-btn copy-btn">Copy</button></div></div>`;
                    token.type = 'html';
                    token.text = `<div class="shiki-container">${header}${shikiHtml}</div>`;
                } else if (token.type === 'codespan') {
                    const raw = await codeToHtml(token.text, { lang: 'text', theme: 'vitesse-dark' });
                    const inline = raw.replace(/<pre[^>]*>/, '').replace('</pre>', '').replace('<code', '<code class="shiki-inline"');
                    token.type = 'html';
                    token.text = inline;
                }
            }
        });

        async function loadMarkdown(path) {
            const response = await fetch(path);
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error('File not found');
            return await response.text();
        }

        function setupShikiInteractions() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.shiki-container').forEach(container => {
                const wrapBtn = container.querySelector('.wrap-btn');
                if (isShikiWrapEnabled) {
                    container.classList.add('wrap-enabled');
                    if (wrapBtn) { wrapBtn.classList.add('active'); wrapBtn.textContent = 'Wrap: On'; }
                } else {
                    if (wrapBtn) wrapBtn.textContent = 'Wrap: Off';
                }
            });
        }
        
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target.matches('.shiki-btn.copy-btn')) {
                const container = e.target.closest('.shiki-container');
                const codeBlock = container?.querySelector('pre.shiki code');
                if (codeBlock) navigator.clipboard.writeText(codeBlock.innerText).then(() => { e.target.textContent = 'Copied!'; setTimeout(() => e.target.textContent = 'Copy', 2000); });
            }
            if (e.target.matches('.shiki-btn.wrap-btn')) {
                isShikiWrapEnabled = !isShikiWrapEnabled;
                localStorage.setItem('shikiWrapEnabled', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                document.querySelectorAll('.shiki-container').forEach(container => {
                    const wrapBtn = container.querySelector('.wrap-btn');
                    container.classList.toggle('wrap-enabled', isShikiWrapEnabled);
                    if (wrapBtn) { wrapBtn.classList.toggle('active', isShikiWrapEnabled); wrapBtn.textContent = isShikiWrapEnabled ? 'Wrap: On' : 'Wrap: Off'; }
                });
            }
        });
        
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
            try {
                const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
                const filePath = params.get('file');
                
                if (!filePath) {
                    document.getElementById('md-content').innerHTML = '<p>No file specified</p>';
                    return;
                }
                
                const markdown = await loadMarkdown('/storage/data/' + filePath);
                document.getElementById('md-content').innerHTML = await marked.parse(markdown);
                setupShikiInteractions();
                
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error loading markdown:', error);
                document.getElementById('md-content').innerHTML = `<p>Error loading file: ${error.message}</p>`;
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

path: Website/storage/internal/pages/projects.html

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Projects - Error Dev</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=JetBrains+Mono:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="/storage/internal/styles/page-styles.css">
    <script src="/storage/internal/scripts/embed-detect.js"></script>
    <script src="/storage/internal/scripts/theme-manager.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/js-yaml/4.1.0/js-yaml.min.js"></script>
</head>
<body>
    <div class="page-container">
        <h1 class="page-title">Projects</h1>
        
        <div class="project-tabs" id="project-tabs"></div>
        
        <div id="tab-container"></div>
    </div>
    
    <script>
        let currentTab = null;

        async function loadYAML(path) {
            const response = await fetch(path);
            const text = await response.text();
            return jsyaml.load(text);
        }

        function renderTabs(tabs) {
            const tabsContainer = document.getElementById('project-tabs');
            
            Object.keys(tabs).forEach(tabKey => {
                const tabData = tabs[tabKey];
                const tabBtn = document.createElement('button');
                tabBtn.className = 'project-tab';
                tabBtn.textContent = tabData.display;
                tabBtn.onclick = () => switchTab(tabKey);
                tabBtn.dataset.tab = tabKey;
                
                tabsContainer.appendChild(tabBtn);
            });
        }

        function renderTabContent(tabKey, tabData) {
            const container = document.getElementById('tab-container');
            
            const tabContent = document.createElement('div');
            tabContent.className = 'tab-content';
            tabContent.dataset.tab = tabKey;
            
            const projectsGrid = document.createElement('div');
            projectsGrid.className = 'projects-grid';
            
            tabData.projects.forEach(project => {
                const card = document.createElement('div');
                card.className = 'project-card';
                
                const title = document.createElement('a');
                title.className = 'project-title';
                title.href = project.link;
                title.target = '_blank';
                title.rel = 'noopener noreferrer';
                title.textContent = project.name;
                
                const description = document.createElement('div');
                description.className = 'project-description';
                description.textContent = project.description;
                
                card.appendChild(title);
                card.appendChild(description);
                projectsGrid.appendChild(card);
            });
            
            tabContent.appendChild(projectsGrid);
            container.appendChild(tabContent);
        }

        function switchTab(tabKey) {
            currentTab = tabKey;
            
            console.log('Switching to tab:', tabKey);
            document.querySelectorAll('.project-tab').forEach(btn => {
                btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.tab === tabKey);
            });
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(content => {
                content.classList.toggle('active', content.dataset.tab === tabKey);
            });
            window.parent.location.hash = `page=projects&tab=${tabKey}`;
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
            try {
                const data = await loadYAML('/storage/data/projects.yaml');
                
                console.log('Projects data loaded:', data);
                
                if (!data || !data.projects || !data.projects.tabs) {
                    console.error('No projects data found');
                    return;
                }
                
                const tabs = data.projects.tabs;
                renderTabs(tabs);
                Object.keys(tabs).forEach(tabKey => {
                    renderTabContent(tabKey, tabs[tabKey]);
                });
                const hash = window.location.hash.substring(1);
                if (hash) {
                    const params = new URLSearchParams(hash);
                    const tab = params.get('tab');
                    
                    if (tab && tabs[tab]) {
                        switchTab(tab);
                    } else {
                        switchTab(Object.keys(tabs)[0]);
                    }
                } else {
                    switchTab(Object.keys(tabs)[0]);
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error loading projects:', error);
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script type="module">
        import { codeToHtml } from 'https://esm.sh/shiki@1.0.0';
        import jsyaml from 'https://esm.sh/js-yaml';

        const card = document.getElementById('main-card');
        const wrapBtn = document.getElementById('wrap-toggle');
        const copyBtn = document.getElementById('copy-btn');
        const langLabel = document.getElementById('lang-label');

        let isWrapped = localStorage.getItem('wordWrap') !== 'false';
        let config = { fileMappings: {}, mapDisplays: {} };

        function updateWrapUI() {
            if (isWrapped) {
                card.classList.add('wrap-enabled');
                wrapBtn.textContent = 'Wrap: On';
                wrapBtn.classList.add('active');
            } else {
                card.classList.remove('wrap-enabled');
                wrapBtn.textContent = 'Wrap: Off';
                wrapBtn.classList.remove('active');
            }
        }

        wrapBtn.onclick = () => {
            isWrapped = !isWrapped;
            localStorage.setItem('wordWrap', isWrapped);
            updateWrapUI();
        };
        function getLangFromFilename(filename) {
            const ext = filename.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            return config.fileMappings[ext] || 'text';
        }
        function getDisplayText(filename, detectedLang) {
            const ext = filename.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();
            const displayName = config.mapDisplays[ext] || detectedLang;
            return displayName.toUpperCase();
        }

        async function init() {
            updateWrapUI();

            const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            const filePath = params.get('file');
            if (!filePath) return;

            try {
                try {
                    const yamlResp = await fetch('/storage/data/raw.yaml');
                    if (yamlResp.ok) {
                        const yamlText = await yamlResp.text();
                        config = jsyaml.load(yamlText) || config;
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    console.warn("raw.yaml not found, using default mappings");
                }

                const response = await fetch('/storage/data/' + filePath);
                if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`File not found: ${filePath}`);
                
                const rawCode = await response.text();
                const lang = getLangFromFilename(filePath);
                langLabel.textContent = getDisplayText(filePath, lang);
                
                const html = await codeToHtml(rawCode, {
                    lang: lang,
                    theme: 'vitesse-dark'
                });

                document.getElementById('code-content').innerHTML = html;

                copyBtn.onclick = () => {
                    navigator.clipboard.writeText(rawCode);
                    const originalText = copyBtn.textContent;
                    copyBtn.textContent = 'Copied!';
                    setTimeout(() => copyBtn.textContent = originalText, 2000);
                };

            } catch (err) {
                console.error(err);
                document.getElementById('code-content').innerHTML = `<p style="padding:2rem; color:#f87171;">Error: ${err.message}</p>`;
            }
        }

        const topBtn = document.getElementById('back-to-top');
        window.onscroll = () => {
            if (window.scrollY > 300) topBtn.classList.add('visible');
            else topBtn.classList.remove('visible');
        };
        topBtn.onclick = () => window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });

        init();
    </script>
</body>

            <script>
                async function fetchGitHubLanguageStats() {
                try {
                    const response = await fetch('https://api.github.com/repos/devicals/devicals.github.io/languages');

                    if (!response.ok) {
                    throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`);
                    }

                    const languages = await response.json();
                    const totalBytes = Object.values(languages).reduce((sum, bytes) => sum + bytes, 0);

                    const languageStats = Object.entries(languages)
                    .map(([language, bytes]) => ({
                        language,
                        percentage: ((bytes / totalBytes) * 100).toFixed(1)
                    }))
                    .sort((a, b) => parseFloat(b.percentage) - parseFloat(a.percentage));

                    const statsString = languageStats
                    .map(({ language, percentage }) => `${language}: ${percentage}%`)
                    .join(', ');

                    return statsString;

                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('Error fetching GitHub language stats:', error);
                    return 'HTML: 95.1%, JS: 0.2%, CSS: 4.7%';
                }
                }

                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', updateLanguageStats);
            </script>
        </div>

        const container = document.getElementById('items-container');

        function validateInput(input) {
            const regex = /^[a-z_:\/]*$/;
            if (!regex.test(input.value)) {
                input.value = input.value.replace(/[^a-z_:\/]/g, '');
            }
        }

        function updateDataState(itemNum) {
            const itemInput = document.getElementById(`i${itemNum}`);
            const dataInput = document.getElementById(`d${itemNum}`);

            if (itemInput.value.trim() === '') {
                dataInput.disabled = true;
                dataInput.value = '';
            } else {
                dataInput.disabled = false;
            }
        }

        function generate() {
            const items = [];
            const data = [];
            const dataBools = [];
            const isAir = [];

            for (let i = 1; i <= 9; i++) {

                data.push(dataVal);
                dataBools.push(dataVal !== '' ? '1' : '0');
